  function getCmpVendorsCookie(name) {
    var cookieValue = null;
    var value = "; " + document.cookie;
    var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
    if (parts.length === 2) {
        cookieValue = parts.pop().split(";").shift();
    }
    return cookieValue;

<script>
    function subscribeToChannels(channels, success, error){
        success = (typeof success == 'function') ? success : function(){};
        error = (typeof error == 'function') ? error : function(){};
        navigator.indigitall.subscribe(channels, success, error);
    }
    function success (success){
        console.log (success);
    }
    function error (error){
        console.log (error);
    }

    document.addEventListener('indigitallReady', function() {
        var defaultChannels = ['actualidad'];
        navigator.indigitall.loadIndigitall('/indigitall/',function(){
            subscribeToChannels(defaultChannels);
        });
    });

</script>
